 What is 'solar eclipse'? The Earth revolves around the Sun and the Moon revolves around the Earth
 parikrama ke dauraan ek duusare ke bich main ye aate jate rahete hai
 When the moon comes between the sun and the earth, it is called a solar eclipse
 iskaa asar prithvi or prithvi ke logon par padataa he
 We have told you what solar eclipse is and how this astronomical event is, but now let you tell what is special in this time of solar eclipse
 
 
 
 Special in 'solar eclipse' - solar eclipse morning 4
 49 se 10
 Looks up to 04 o'clock
 - yah surya grahan bharat main aanshik rup se dikhaai de rahaa he
 - The total duration of solar eclipse in India is 30 minutes and the eclipse takes place in Aquarius sign
 surya grahan kaa saamaanya prabhaav- is grahan main surya kaa sanyog ketu se ban rahaa he

 - surya or ketu kaa prabhaav hone se durghatnaon kii sambhaavna ban rahi he

 - brihaspati kii najar bhi he isliye upaay karne se laabh hoga

 to kul milakar dekhen to jyotishi maanate hai ki saamanyataur parasurya grahan kaa bura asar hi hamaare upar padataa he, lekin kuch upayon ko apana kar surya grahan ke prabhaav se bachaa ja saktaa he

 - surya grahan ke dauraan mantra jaap or dhyaan karnaa sarvottam hota he

 co / pngyo4xn9uto people who are commenting on my morning tweets,they were made before the verdict ! Thoughts n prayers Makar Sakranti is also one of the most sacred religious ceremonies of the Hindus
 is din shraddhalu pavitra nadiyon main dubkee lagaakar samast paapon se mukti pate hai
 The festival of Makar Sakranti is celebrated in almost the entire country
 14 janvari or kuch jagahon par 13-15 janvari tak yah tyohaar manaaya jaataa he
 It is known by different names in different states and there are different ways of celebrating it
 uttarakhand ke pahaado main makar sakranti ke tyohaar kii raunak hi kuch or hoti he
 According to the Hindu calendar, Makar Sankranti is celebrated to commemorate the entry of Makar from the Sun's Cancer zodiac
 is din ko ritu parivartan ke rup main dekha jaataa he
 It is believed that from the day of Makar Sankranti, the sun starts moving slowly towards the north
 dhire-dhire din bade hone lagate hai or garmi bhi badhane lagati he
 With this, migratory birds also turn back to the colder regions of the mountains
 uttarakhand ke kumaun kshetra main ise ‘uttarayani’ or ‘ghughti sagyaan’ ke naam se bhi janaa jaataa he, jabaki gadhwal main ‘khichdi sakranti’ kaha jaataa he
 On this day fairs are organized here
 kaale kauwa kaale
 
 
 In Kumaon, flour ghughut, dates etc
 are made on this day, while in Garhwal it is customary to eat khichdi and donate
 kumaun main kauwe ko ghughut khilaane kaa rivaaj he or iske liye kauwe ko ‘kaale kauwa kaale, ghughti maala khale’ gaakar bulaayaa jaataa he
 Different shapes are made from it by adding fennel, gud etc
 to the flour and after some time it is dried and fry in ghee, these are called ghughut
 bachche ghughut kii maala banaakar or use gale main daalkar gaanv bhar main ghoomte-phirte hai
 In Garhwal, urad dal khichdi is made on this day and there is also the custom of blowing pantang
 is din brahmanon ko urad daal or chaaval daan karne kaa rivaaj bhi gadhwal main he
 It is also called Chuniya festival in villages, where Malpuve (chuniya) is made with special type of flour on this day
 uttarayani melamkar sakranti ke maukey par uttarakhand main jagah-jagah uttarayani melon kaa aayojan hota he
 People from both Kumaon and Garhwal regions eagerly await the Uttarayani fair
 bageshwar kaa uttarayani mela to duniyabar main prasiddh he
 Apart from Bageshwar, Uttarayani fairs are also worth seeing in Haridwar, Rudraprayag, Pauri and Nainital districts
 bageshwar-uttarayani mela:bageshwar main sarayu or gomti nadi ke tat par bhagwaan shiv ke bagnath mandir ke paas is meley kaa bhavy aayojan hota he
 It is believed that by taking a bath in the confluence day, all sins are cut
 kitne din kaa aayojan:bageshwar main uttarayani mela 1 hafte tak chalata he
 How far: To reach Bageshwar, the nearest Pantnagar Airport is about 180 km from here in Udham Singh Nagar district

 kuch pramukh shaharon se bageshwar kii duuri

 yah mela saanskrithik aayojanon or vyapaar kaa centre hota he

 1921 main samajasevakon ne badhua mazdooree ke unmoolan ke liye yaheen se hunkaar bhari thi, jise aaj bhi ‘kuli begaar’ naam se janaa jaataa he
